Giai \u0111o\u1ea1n T\u00e1i t\u00edch lu\u1ef9 (Re-Accumulation)\n\nGiai \u0111o\u1ea1n tho\u00e1i lui tr\u01b0\u1edbc halving \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c theo sau b\u1edfi giai \u0111o\u1ea1n t\u00e1i t\u00edch lu\u1ef9 k\u00e9o d\u00e0i trong nhi\u1ec1u th\u00e1ng (m\u00e0u \u0111\u1ecf)\n\nNhi\u1ec1u nh\u00e0 \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 b\u1ecb lo\u1ea1i b\u1ecf trong giai \u0111o\u1ea1n n\u00e0y do s\u1ef1 bu\u1ed3n ch\u00e1n, kh\u00f4ng ki\u00ean nh\u1eabn v\u00e0 th\u1ea5t v\u1ecdng v\u00ec kh\u00f4ng \u0111\u1ea1t \u0111\u01b0\u1ee3c k\u1ebft qu\u1ea3 mong mu\u1ed1n trong \u0111\u1ea7u t\u01b0 BTC c\u1ee7a h\u1ecd ngay sau halving\n\n5. Xu h\u01b0\u1edbng t\u0103ng c\u1ea5p t\u1ed1c (Parabolic Uptrend)\n\nKhi Bitcoin b\u1ee9t ph\u00e1 ra kh\u1ecfi khu v\u1ef1c t\u00e1i t\u00edch lu\u1ef9 v\u00e0 v\u00e0o xu h\u01b0\u1edbng t\u0103ng c\u1ea5p t\u1ed1c (m\u00e0u xanh)\n\nTrong giai \u0111o\u1ea1n n\u00e0y, Bitcoin tr\u1ea3i qua s\u1ef1 t\u0103ng tr\u01b0\u1edfng nhanh ch\u00f3ng tr\u00ean \u0111\u01b0\u1eddng \u0111\u1ebfn c\u00e1c m\u1ee9c gi\u00e1 k\u1ef7 l\u1ee5c m\u1edbi\n\n#Crypto  #Bitcoin", "replyCount": 61, "retweetCount": 3, "likeCount": 74, "quoteCount": 1, "conversationId": 1710540661081198662, "hashtags": ["BTC"], "cashtags": [], "mentionedUsers": [], "links": [], "viewCount": 3346, "retweetedTweet": null, "quotedTweet": null, "place": null, "coordinates": null, "inReplyToTweetId": null, "inReplyToUser": null, "source": "<a href=\"http://twitter.com/download/android\" rel=\"nofollow\">Twitter for Android</a>", "sourceUrl": "http://twitter.com/download/android", "sourceLabel": "Twitter for Android", "media": {"photos": [{"url": "https://pbs.twimg.com/media/F70PqlrbMAAgx9i.jpg"}], "videos": [], "animated": []}, "_type": "snscrape.modules.twitter.Tweet"}
